quyet glad conscience god rom harte beleued ryghtwysnes pronounceth faythe iustice harte gal no christo hesu credim vt iustificem ex fide christi et non ex operibus legis beleue christ iesu may iustified fayth christ nat workes lawe ephe gratia enim saluati estis per fidem et hoc ex vobis dei enim donum est non ex operibus ne quis glorietur grace ye saued faythe nat selues gyft god workes leaste man shulde glorie authority gospel iohan ioha dedit eis potestatem filios dei fieri qui credunt nomine eius qui non ex sanguimbus ne que ex voluntate carnis ne que ex voluntate viri sed ex deo nati sunt gaue power becum chyldren god meane whiche beleue name whiche borne nat blodes neyther wyl fleshe neyther wyl man god ioh sient moses exaltauit serpetem deserto ita exaltari oportet filium hominis vt omnis qui credit ipsum non pereat lykewese moses exalted serpent desert must sone man exalted whiche beleue hym peryshe nat also non misit deus filium sunin mundum vt iudicet mudum sed vt saluetur mundus per ipsum qui credit eum non indicatur god set nat son worlde yt shulde iudge world yt worlde shulde saued hym beleueth hym nat iudged authority actes apostle actes notum igitur sit vobis viri fratres per hunc vobis remissio peccatorum annunciatur c knowen therfore vnto brethern remission synnes preached vnto al tho thinges ye coulde nat iustified lawe hym beleueth iustifyed howe myght clearely spoken office christe iustifycacyon lawe quod iustifyed nat therfore christe gyuen shuld beleue iustified openly plucketh fro lawe iustifycacyon ergo christe accompted iuste whan beleue god pacified v hym act stone disallowed buylders whiche made cornerstone nat helth none name vnder heuen gyuen vnto men ought saued name christ sticked fayth ergo truste name nat trust work saued name mercifull addeth fayth viuifyeth fayth genderethin harte peace ioy euerlastynge lyfe esa noticia eius iudicabit multos prophet esaye knowledge hi shall iudge many knowledge christ knowe benefit aucthorytes testymonyes otherwhiles sheweth lawe otherwhyles promyses chryst remyssyon synnes free acceptaunce chryste authorites doctours also amonge holye father spred many lyke testymonyes saynt ambrose sayth hys epystle ireneus thus subditus autem mundus eo per legem factus est quia ex prescripto legis omnes conueniuntur et ex operibus legis nemo iustificatur saynte ambrose id est quia per legem peccatum cognoscitur sed culpa non relaxatur videbatur lex nocuisse que omnes fecerat peccatores sed veniens dominus iesus peccatuz omnib quod nemo poterat euitare donauit et chirographum nostru sui sanguinis effusione deleuit hoc est quod ait abundauit peccatu per legem superabundauit autem gratia per iesum quia postqua totus mundus subditus factus est totius mudi peccatum abstulit sicut testificatus est iohannes dice ecce agnus dei ecce qui tollit peccatu mundi et ideo nemo glorietur operibus quia nemo factis suis instificatur sed qui instus est donatum habet quia post lauacrum iustificatus est fides ergo est que liberat per sanguinem christi quia beatus ille cui peccatum remittitur et venia donatur saye world made subiect therfore lawe prescript lawe al conuented hyghe iudge workes lawe iustifyed lawe synne knowen offence remytted lawe semed haue hurted whiche made men synners lorde iesus comyng pardoned unto al men synne whiche man coulde eschewe dyd clene stryke chirografe shedyng blode thys sayeth syn aboundaunt lawe grace iesus aboundant hole worlde become subiecte toke away sinne hole worlde testifieth iohan saing lo lambe god lo taketh awaye syn worlde therfore lette man glorye hys workes man iustyfyed hy hys factes iustifyed hath gyuen wherfore fayth thynge delyuereth bloude chryste blyssed synne remytted pardone gyuen wordes saynt ambrose apertly defende opinion plucketh awaye workes iustificacyon gyueth faythe delyuereth bloude chryste let sentenciaryes layde together heape furnyshed neuer gloryous tytles called angelycal seraphical subtyle irrefragable red red agayne shal make moche vnderstandynge paule thys one sentence saynte ambrose dothe saynte austyns lyke sentence wryteth also saynte austyne moche agaynste pelagyans hys boke de spiritu et litera saythe thus ideo quippe proponitur iusticia legis qui fecerit ea viuet illa vt cum quis que infirmitatem suam cognouerit non per suas vires ne que per literam ipsius legis quod fieri non potest sed per fidem concilians iustificatorem perueniat et faciat et viuat eam opus rectum quod qui fecerit viuit eo non fit nisi iustificato iustificatio autem ex fide impetratur therfore timentibus penam absconditur gratia sub quo timore anima laborans c per fidem confugiat ad misericordiam dei vt det quod iubet saye lawe feare god fayth truste god feare payne grace hyd whiche feare vndoubted worde god whiche oughte teache accordyng vse theyr iurisdiction wherfore folowith nat although haue iurisdiction may institute newe honour seruices ceremony seruices nothynge apperteyne iurisdiction haue worde co maundement howe farre forthe ought excercise theyr iurisdiction whiche man haue comitted trespassed agaynst worde whiche haue receiued christe howbeit cofession haue added
